If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
specify the full pathname of the library, or use the `-LLIBDIR'
flag during linking and do at least one of the following:
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_LIBRARY_PATH' environment variable
     during execution
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable
     during linking
   - use the `-Wl,-rpath -Wl,LIBDIR' linker flag
   - have your system administrator add LIBDIR to `/etc/ld.so.conf'

See any operating system documentation about shared libraries for
more information, such as the ld(1) and ld.so(8) manual pages.

	    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < moonshot-ui.po > moonshot-ui.2po && \
	    if cmp moonshot-ui.1po moonshot-ui.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
	      rm -f moonshot-ui.1po moonshot-ui.2po moonshot-ui.po; \
	    else \
	      rm -f moonshot-ui.1po moonshot-ui.2po ./moonshot-ui.pot && \
	      mv moonshot-ui.po ./moonshot-ui.pot; \
	    fi; \
	  else \
	    mv moonshot-ui.po ./moonshot-ui.pot; \
	  fi; \
	}
